***картавить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картавить.html>карта́вить</a> (28437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картавить.html>карта́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to burr, to mispronounce some sounds, to especially [r] and, to less commonly [l]</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>ка́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <span>приставочные <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a></span> закартавить, накартавить, покартавить, прокартавить, скартавить.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-картав-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***картина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a> (621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cartina</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fine paper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>picture (representation of visible reality produced by drawing, etc.)</li>
<li>painting, canvas</li>
<li>movie, film</li>
<li>picture, image (as produced in transient fashion by technology, e.g. a monitor)</li>
<li>scene</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>For sense 1, this term is often used in the sense of referring to a painting created by hand and perceived as a work of art. On the other hand, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нка</a></i> is preferably used for photographs and other non-transient images created with the help of technology.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="checksense">
<dl><dd><i>The terms below need to be checked and allocated to the definitions (senses) of the headword above. Each term should appear in the sense for which it is appropriate. Use the templates <code> |  | syn | ru | ... |  | </code> or <code> |  | ant | ru | ... |  | </code> to add them to the appropriate sense(s).</i></dd></dl>
</div>

***картинка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нка</a> (2926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинка.html>карти́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: a small picture, photograph or illustration; icon</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This term is typically used in a general fashion to refer to images, photographs etc., with a tendency of usage for creations that were made with the help of technology. In terms of refering to drawings, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a></i> is mainly used for hand-made paintings and often carries a sense of referring to a perceived work of art.
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>ка́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тина.html>ти́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинный.html>карти́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картинно.html>карти́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartínno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-карти́нно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)карти́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-карти́нно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)карти́нней</b>)

<ol><li>expressively</li>

</p>

<li>expressive</li>
<li>picturesque</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́н</a> (12393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">carton</i> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Karton</i>, both borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cartone</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картон.html>карто́нов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картонный.html>карто́нный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cardboard, paperboard</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картотека.html>картоте́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartotéka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картотека.html>картоте́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картотека.html>картоте́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картотека.html>картоте́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>file cabinet, document cabinet, card index</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кара.html>ка́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картошка.html>карто́шка</a> (2014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">карто́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartóxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a dialectal form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картофель.html>карто́фель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartófelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Recorded since the middle of the 19th century. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">карто́(фель)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kartó(felʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***картуз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:картуз.html>карту́з</a> (13010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картуз.html>карту́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kartúz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картуз.html>карту́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картуз.html>карту́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картуз.html>карту́зов</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">карту́зик</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>type of a peaked cap with high cap band</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> paper bag for various loose materials</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> powder bag</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карусель.html>карусе́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karusélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карусель.html>карусе́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карусель.html>карусе́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карусель.html>карусе́лей</a></b>)

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерист.html>карьери́ст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">karʹjeríst</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерист.html>карьери́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерист.html>карьери́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:карьерист.html>карьери́стов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> careerist; social climber</li></ol>

***касаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́ться</a> (991)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">касатисѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kasatisę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kasati</i> + reflexive <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sę</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kasátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коснуться.html>косну́ться</a></b>) (+ genitive case)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́емся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кончик.html>ко́нчиком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языка́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верхний.html>ве́рхней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губы́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kasájemsja</b> kónčikom jazyká vérxnej gubý.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We touch the upper lip with the tip of the tongue. (from "<a href = vnd.unilang:малыш.html>Малыш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>у́чится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a> - The baby is learning to speak" by Anna Gerasimova)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to concern, to have to do with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:касаться.html>каса́ется</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto tebjá ne <b>kasájetsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This doesn't concern you.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">touch</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">trógatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дотрагиваться.html>дотра́гиваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dotrágivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***каскад.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́д</a> (22546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaskád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́дов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">каска́дный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cascade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́д</a></b> гидроэлектроста́нций</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaskád</b> gidroelektrostáncij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">series of hydroelectric power plants; coordinated hydroelectric system</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красноречие.html>красноре́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaskád</b> krasnoréčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flood of eloquence</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">radio</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каскад.html>каска́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:усиление.html>усиле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaskád</b> usilénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">amplifier/gain stage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">operetta</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> song and dance number</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">circus</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stunt sequence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figure skating</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jump combination</li></ol>

***каспийский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каспийский.html>каспи́йский</a> (21522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Caspius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Caspian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́йский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каспийский.html>каспи́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaspíjskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Caspian

***кассационный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кассационный.html>кассацио́нный</a> (32024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kassation</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">касса́ция</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kassácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кассационный.html>кассацио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kassaciónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> appeal, cassation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кассационный.html>кассацио́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалоба.html>жа́лоба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kassaciónnaja</b> žáloba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">appeal</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>кас<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>са<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ци<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>о́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-касс-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-аци-онн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
